21/08/15, 10:38 PM - Rahul Kumar: An SIG (Special Interest Group) is by students and for students. It is not a workshop. Rather it is skill development course that goes on whole Sem. One class every week.

You can learn about the principles of Aerospace ( a new SIG started this year), or the basics of architecture and programming AVR of Microcontrollers, or learn a modern and general purpose programming language called Python ( with separate classes for people who know programming and those who are new to it.) 

So if you are interested, send in a application for an SIG of your choice.
Who knows, you may do projects in that field; or maybe, even teach it next time!

Open for both IEEE member and non members.

Register at
http://www.bmsceieee.com/joinsig.html

08/09/15, 8:41 PM - Omkar: In Japan, in a soap manufacturing company the soap blocks were made,
then wrapped in a wrapping paper automatically on an assembly conveyer belt
and finally packed in cartons...

Many a times it happened that the wrapping machine wrapped the paper without soap. i.e. you had an empty packet without soap.

To rectify this problem the Japanese company bought a X-ray scanner from the US for $60,000 to check on the  assembly line whether the container contained soap and wasn't empty.  


A similar problem happened at Nirma soaps, in Ahmedabad in INDIA.. Guess what they did????

They bought a bajaj fan costing around Rs.1500/- and placed it on the edge of the assembly line.
The empty wrappers, without soaps just blew away!!!

Hey guys, I'm from 8th sem ISE. I got placed after attending 50 companies. I don't want my juniors to struggle like me. So here's few advices I would like to give.ğŸ˜‹

â€¢Never study subjects for marks. You need to have strong basic knowledge in all the subjects. not jus one subject.

â€¢Stop running behind GPA. 
If you have 8.5 and above, you can attend all the companies. 
If you have 8 and above you eligible for 90% of the companies. 
Above 7, you can atleast attend mass recruiters. 
If you have more than two backlogs, you have a tuff time in placements.

â€¢Important subjects. 
C C++ Java DBMS OS UNIX
Whether you are in IS/CS or any other branch you have to learn these subjects. Every company loves asking these 6 subjects.

â€¢Non IS/CS branches. 
Chances of you ppl getting into your core companies is very less. May be 10%. Rest all will end up in IT companies. So, atleast be strong in one programming language and one theory subject of IS/CS branch. ğŸ˜•

â€¢Lucky Bastards (IS/CS)
If BMSCE gets 150 companies, you will be eligible for 120+ companies. Everyone in the college will be jealous of you guys. ğŸ˜ˆ

â€¢Top companies
Kirusa(20lakhs per annum)
Nutanix(19lpa)
Urban laddar(16lpa)
And another 20 companies above 10lpa. ğŸ˜

â€¢Mass recruiters
IS/CS students, its advisable not to sit for these. it might take long time to get placed in non-mass recruiters. If you believe in yourself, you need not attend mass recruiters. If you don't want to take risk, you can attend it. Give chance for other branch guys to get placed noğŸ˜œ

â€¢Tips to get placed in mass recruiters. 
Do not have more than one backlog. 
CGPA 7.5 and above. 
Strong communication knowledge. Strong aptitude skills. 
That's it. You will be placedğŸ˜‚

â€¢Mass recruiters package
TCS(3.2lpa) -hired 230 students 
Accenture (3.5lpa)-150 students
Wipro(3.2lpa)-40 students.

â€¢Start preparing
Every company will have their first round as Aptitude round. 
Practice verbal, non verbal and quantitative questions. If you don't clear this round, you can't get placed anywhere. 
Buy RS Agarwal book(Bible) 
www.indiabix.com
Start practicing from now itself. Remember, this is VERY VERY important.

â€¢Coding 
whether you are in IS/CS or others,If you want higher package, you need to be strong in coding. Very strong
Practice in 
www.hackerrank.com
Codechef. Com
Hackerearth.com 
You want 10lpa and above, be strong in coding.

â€¢My seniors nor lecturers gave us suggestions before. I'm giving you ppl now itself because I don't want you people to struggle for placements like me.

â€¢BMSCE gets nearly 150 companies. You will get placed for sure. Have patience til the end and never lose hope. ğŸ˜

01/03/16, 9:56 PM - Srinivas Kumar R, CS BMSCE: Pls do not ignore or delay reading this:

When lights are off at night, one must not view the hand phone! (Smartphone)

Please share with family friends URGENTLY.....

Habitually using hand phones before bedtime in the dark can lead to serious problems.

Recently, an increasing number of 30-40 year-old patients are seeking medical attention due to using hand phones in the dark.

Professor Li Li, director of the Hospital of Ophthalmology SGH Singapore, said: direct glare of >30 minutes would cause irreversible eye macular degeneration that leads to rapid deterioration of vision.

Contracting maculopathy (eye cancer) means waiting for loss of sight because modern medicine cannot treat, let alone cure it.
The bright phone in the dark with close-up view high-energy directed at the eyes will damage the macula of the eye.

Professor Li Li said that symptoms of macular degeneration is mostly experienced by old people, but lately patients are getting younger. Patients who are 30-40 years of age increased by 3 %, most are frequent users of hand phones.

However, viewing the hand phone in the dark not only causes macular degeneration. It initially causes dry eyes, cataracts and eventually loss of sight.

Early lesions of the eye have to be treated with laser or injection of steroids.

254 Hospital eye specialist Professor Li Li suggested that the most important thing is to get rid of the bad habit of using hand phones in the dark. Because habitual use of hand phones in the dark before bedtime may cause a lifetime of harm.

Friends : In order to look after ourselves and our families, remember not to turn off the lights if viewing the hand phone. Inform hand phone users urgently that viewing hand phones in the dark can easily lead to loss of sight!
